本文系统研究了大型视觉-语言模型中基于提示的验证方法，发现其效果依赖于输入难度：对困难样本有帮助，但对简单样本可能有害；据此提出无需训练的风险感知选择性提示方法（RSP），利用生成前不确定性信号选择性地触发验证。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 尽管基于提示的验证被广泛用于缓解大型视觉-语言模型中的幻觉问题，但该方法何时有效、何时可能失效的机制尚不清晰，现有研究缺乏对其风险与收益的系统性理解。

**Method:** 本文系统研究了两种代表性LVLM架构上的验证提示方法，分析了其在不同难度输入下的校正与引入错误的行为模式；进一步通过注意力分布与中间层熵模式分析了验证提示的内部机制；并提出了无需训练的Risk-aware Selective Prompting（RSP）方法，利用生成前的不确定性信号来有选择地触发验证。

**Result:** 实验表明，验证提示的校正效果随输入难度增加而提升，但新引入的错误在不同难度下持续存在，导致始终开启的验证对困难输入有效，但容易对简单输入造成损害；RSP方法在保持基线性能的同时缓解了始终提示的退化，且最优的选择性信号因架构而异。

**Conclusion:** 验证提示是一种有风险的干预手段，其有效性取决于输入难度，这种行为与保守化输出偏移以及注意力从视觉令牌向指令令牌的重新分配有关；RSP提供了一种训练免费的高效替代方案，提示未来工作需根据架构特性设计选择性验证策略。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Prompt-based verification is widely used to mitigate hallucinations in large vision-language models (LVLMs), yet when it helps remains poorly understood. We systematically study verification prompting across two representative LVLM architectures and hallucination benchmarks, and find that it is a risk-bearing intervention: its corrections increase with input difficulty, while newly introduced errors persist across difficulty levels. As a result, always-on prompting helps on hard inputs but offers little benefit -- and can harm -- easier ones. Our analysis further shows that this behavior is associated with a conservative output shift. Verification prompts redistribute attention from visual tokens toward instruction tokens and induce a distinct middle-layer entropy pattern absent in a neutral-prompt control, suggesting instruction-conditioned attention redistribution rather than uniformly improved visual grounding. Motivated by this input-dependent risk, we propose Risk-aware Selective Prompting (RSP), a training-free approach that uses pre-generation uncertainty signals to trigger verification selectively. RSP mitigates the degradation of always-on prompting while preserving baseline performance, and reveals that effective selection signals vary across architectures.


### [74] [Pruning and Distilling Mixture-of-Experts into Dense Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28207)
*Junhyuck Kim, Jihun Yun, Haechan Kim, Gyeongman Kim, Joonghyun Bae, Jaewoong Cho*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出首个将混合专家模型（MoE）系统性地转换为标准全稠密架构的框架，通过专家评分、选择和分组、拼接为稠密前馈网络并经过知识蒸馏精炼，在Qwen3-30B-A3B等模型上验证了350种配置，发现多样性感知评分方法效果最优，且在参数匹配条件下MoE转稠密相比稠密剪枝在下游准确率上平均提升6.3个百分点，训练速度快1.6倍。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** MoE虽是前沿语言模型的主流架构，但其所有专家参数必须常驻内存，因此在内存受限的部署场景下不够理想；现有压缩方法虽减少了专家数量，但输出仍是MoE模型，未能从根本上解决内存占用问题。

**Method:** 提出首个将训练好的MoE转换为标准全稠密架构的系统性框架：对专家进行评分、选择和分组，然后拼接为稠密前馈网络，并通过来自MoE教师的知识蒸馏进行精炼；在Qwen3-30B-A3B上评估了7种评分方法、5种分组方法和2种幅度缩放方法，共350种配置。

**Result:** 评分方法的选择影响最大，新提出的多样性感知评分在Qwen3-30B-A3B、DeepSeek-V2-Lite和GPT-OSS-20B上持续优于此前方法；在参数匹配的受控比较下，MoE转稠密在下游平均准确率上比稠密剪枝高出6.3个百分点，且经过约4B token的蒸馏后训练墙钟速度快1.6倍。

**Conclusion:** MoE转稠密是一种可行且高效的部署优化策略，在同等参数规模下优于传统的稠密剪枝方法，为内存受限场景下的MoE模型部署提供了新的方向，且框架中评分方法的选择是关键设计因素。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) is now the dominant architecture for frontier language models, yet it requires all expert parameters to be loaded in memory, making it less preferable for memory-constrained deployment. Existing compression methods reduce the number of experts but the output remains an MoE model with the same fundamental limitation. We present the first systematic framework for converting a trained MoE into a standard fully dense architecture: experts are scored, selected, and grouped, then concatenated into a dense FFN and refined by knowledge distillation from the MoE teacher. We evaluate 7 scoring, 5 grouping, and 2 magnitude scaling methods across a range of selected expert counts on Qwen3-30B-A3B, yielding 350 configurations. We find that the choice of scoring method is the most impactful, with our novel diversity-aware scoring consistently outperforming prior methods on Qwen3-30B-A3B, DeepSeek-V2-Lite, and GPT-OSS-20B. Under a controlled comparison at matched parameter count, MoE-to-dense outperforms dense-to-dense pruning by +6.3 pp in average downstream accuracy after ~4B-token distillation at 1.6x faster training wall-clock speed.


### [75] [Analyzing Quality-Latency-Resource Trade-offs in a Technical Documentation RAG Assistant Using LoRA Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28222)
*Evgenii Palnikov, Elizaveta Gavrilova*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文系统研究了基于LoRA的文档检索增强生成系统在质量、延迟和资源之间的权衡，通过人工验证的Kubernetes文档基准测试和20种LoRA配置消融实验发现，仅作用于q和v注意力投影的LoRA适配器在帕累托前沿上持续占优，且该优势是结构性的而非单纯的参数数量所致。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有研究缺乏对文档检索增强生成系统中生成器采用低秩适配（LoRA）时质量、延迟和资源三者之间系统性的权衡分析，尤其是不同LoRA配置（秩和目标模块选择）对整体性能的影响尚未被全面量化研究。

**Method:** 构建了包含5,144个问答对的人工验证Kubernetes文档基准，结合固定混合检索管道（BGE-M3稠密检索、BGE-M3原生稀疏检索、互惠排名融合、交叉编码器重排序），在Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct和Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct两个基座上对20种LoRA配置（不同秩和目标模块选择）进行消融实验，评估指标包括token级F1、LLM评判的根基性（groundedness）和正确性（pass@4）、推理延迟、推理内存及训练成本，所有指标均使用bootstrap 95%置信区间报告。

**Result:** 帕累托分析表明仅作用于q和v注意力投影的LoRA适配器在帕累托前沿上持续占据优势，3B/8B模型选择主要决定了系统的运行区间；参数匹配的对照实验进一步证明q/v优势是结构性的而非单纯的参数量优势。

**Conclusion:** 该研究为RAG系统中LoRA适配器的设计选择提供了明确的经验指导：优先选择仅对q和v投影进行低秩适配的配置可在质量-延迟-资源之间取得最优权衡，同时揭示了模型规模选择与适配器结构设计在系统工程中的不同作用层次。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We study quality-latency-resource trade-offs in a documentation-grounded retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) system that uses Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) of the generator. We build a manually verified benchmark of 5,144 question-answer pairs over the official Kubernetes documentation and combine it with a fixed hybrid-retrieval pipeline (BGE-M3 dense, BGE-M3 native sparse, Reciprocal Rank Fusion, cross-encoder reranking). Over this benchmark we ablate 20 LoRA configurations on Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct and Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct across rank and target-module choices, and evaluate each on token-level F1, LLM-judged groundedness and correctness (pass@4), inference latency, inference memory, and training cost, all reported with bootstrap 95% confidence intervals. Pareto analysis shows that LoRA adapters acting only on the q and v attention projections consistently dominate the front, while the 3B/8B choice mainly defines operating regime. A param-matched control comparison further indicates that the q/v advantage is structural rather than purely parametric. The benchmark, selected adapters, and code are available at https://github.com/EugPal/rag-lora-tradeoffs.


### [76] [Routing-Aligned Fine-Tuning for Multilingual Downstream Tasks in Mixture-of-Experts Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28306)
*Guanzhi Deng, Kuan Wu, Haibo Wang, Shing Yin Wong, Sichun Luo, Linqi Song*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
RA-MoE提出了一种面向混合专家模型的三阶段微调框架，通过发现中间层的语言通用对齐区域并引入路由对齐损失，显著提升了MoE模型在非英语下游任务上的性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有MoE模型的微调方法将其视为整体学习器，忽略了预训练过程中形成的异构路由结构，导致模型在非英语下游任务上的适应能力受限。

**Method:** RA-MoE包含三个阶段：首先将并行任务样本按英语和目标语言的正确性分为四类（cc/ci/ic/ii）；然后定位中间层中任务相关的专家；最后在标准SFT基础上引入路由对齐损失，鼓励ci类型样本在目标语言上的路由跟随英语任务专家的激活模式。

**Result:** 在三种MoE模型、三种任务和六种目标语言上的实验表明，RA-MoE一致优于标准SFT及Routing Steering、RISE等强基线方法，且ci比例可作为对齐收益的可靠预测指标。

**Conclusion:** 中间层形成了语言通用的对齐区域，其路由分歧能够预测跨语言性能差距，基于这一发现设计的路由对齐微调策略可有效提升MoE模型的多语言任务适应能力。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models have emerged as a dominant paradigm for efficient LLM scaling, yet adapting them to non-English downstream tasks remains challenging. Existing fine-tuning approaches treat MoE models as monolithic learners, ignoring the heterogeneous routing structure that develops during pretraining. We validate across multiple MoE models and downstream tasks that middle layers form a language-universal alignment zone where routing divergence strongly predicts per-language task performance gaps. Building on this observation, we propose RA-MoE (Routing-Aligned MoE Fine-Tuning), a three-stage framework that categorizes parallel task examples into a four-way taxonomy (cc/ci/ic/ii) based on correctness in English and the target language, identifies task-relevant experts in the middle layers, and augments standard SFT with a routing alignment loss that encourages target-language routing on ci-type examples to follow the English task-expert activation pattern. Experiments across three MoE models, three tasks, and six target languages demonstrate that RA-MoE consistently outperforms standard SFT and strong baselines including Routing Steering and RISE, with the ci proportion of a task-language pair serving as a reliable predictor of alignment benefit.


### [77] [When Discourse Pressures Conflict: Information Structure in Vision-Language Model Outputs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28346)
*Marcell Fekete, Johannes Bjerva, Tamás Káldi*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文研究视觉语言模型（VLM）是否能像人类一样根据信息结构（IS）区分话语旧信息（Topic）和新信息（Focus），通过匈牙利语中Topic和Focus映射到特定句法位置这一特性进行实验。结果表明VLM虽能产生IS相关结构，但存在过度正则化现象，趋于使用单一响应模板而非人类的多样化策略，提示VLM评估应关注内容在话语中的组织形式而不仅仅是内容准确性。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有VLM评估主要关注模型是否识别正确的视觉内容，但很少考察模型是否以符合话语语境的形式表达这些内容。本文利用信息结构（IS）这一语言学理论，填补这一研究空白，专门检验VLM是否能区分话语旧信息（Topic）和话语新信息（Focus）。

**Method:** 本研究利用匈牙利语中Topic和Focus映射到特定句法位置的特性，使IS选择在文本中可直接观察。实验比较了六种VLM与人类参与者在视觉问答任务中的表现，分析模型在话语状态、语法角色（主语倾向作为Topic）和指称性（不定指倾向作为Focus）等多重压力下的IS实现策略。

**Result:** 六种VLM均能产生IS相关句法结构，但表现出过度正则化现象，与人类在话语状态、语法角色和指称性多重交互压力下选择多样化IS实现策略不同，VLM倾向于收敛到单一的窄响应模板，类似于模式崩溃（mode collapse）现象。

**Conclusion:** VLM评估应超越内容准确性，关注内容如何为话语语境进行信息包装。模型对IS的过度正则化表明其在语用理解和生成多样性方面与人类存在显著差距，需要更全面的评估框架来考察模型的话语能力。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision-language models (VLMs) are increasingly evaluated for whether they identify the right visual content, but little is known about whether they express such content in a discourse-appropriate form. We address this research gap using information structure (IS), testing whether VLMs distinguish discourse-old Topics from discourse-new Foci in visually grounded question answering. We exploit Hungarian, a language in which Topic and Focus map onto dedicated syntactic positions, making IS choices observable in text. Comparing six VLMs with human participants, we find that models produce IS-relevant constructions, but over-regularise this sensitivity. Under the interacting pressures of discourse status, grammatical role (preference for subject Topics) and definiteness (preference for indefinite Foci), humans choose variable strategies for IS realisation. VLMs, by contrast, collapse onto narrow response templates, resembling mode collapse (Kirk et al., 2024). Our findings suggest that VLM evaluation should look beyond content accuracy to how content is packaged for the discourse.


### [78] [Skill0.5: Joint Skill Internalization and Utilization for Out-of-Distribution Generalization in Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28424)
*Jiapeng Zhu, Jianxiang Yu, Yibo Zhao, Chengcheng Han, Qi Gu, Xunliang Cai, Xiang Li, Weining Qian*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出Skill0.5框架，通过将通用技能内化与任务特定技能外化相结合，并借助难度感知路由器进行动态任务分级的优化策略，在兼顾泛化能力与执行效率的同时，解决了现有基于技能的强化学习方法中完全外化带来的上下文开销与完全内化导致的过拟合及知识冲突问题。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有基于技能的强化学习方法在技能处理上存在两难困境：完全外化（即技能显式存储在上下文中）会导致巨大的上下文开销，而完全内化（即技能隐式编码在模型参数中）则容易引发过拟合和知识冲突，缺乏一种能够兼顾二者优点并避免各自缺陷的技能差异化处理机制。

**Method:** 提出Skill0.5框架，这是一个明确的技能差异化强化学习框架，其核心是一个动态难度感知路由器，将任务流划分为不同的掌握等级并应用定制化优化策略：对于困难任务，通过特权蒸馏（privileged distillation）将通用技能内化，建立认知基础；对于简单任务，则通过诊断探针（diagnostic probing）惩罚捷径行为并强制使用特定技能，从而实现通用技能内化与任务特定技能外化的有机结合。

**Result:** 在ALFWorld和WebShop环境上的实验表明，Skill0.5在分布内和分布外场景下均优于基于记忆和基于技能的强化学习基线方法，取得了显著的性能提升。

**Conclusion:** 该研究证明了在基于技能的大语言模型智能体中，对通用技能和任务特定技能采取差异化处理策略（内化与外化的结合）是有效的，为构建更高效、更鲁棒的可自主智能体提供了新的范式，并指出了动态任务路由与定制化优化在技能学习中的关键作用。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Equipping large language models with explicit skills has emerged as a promising paradigm for enabling autonomous agents to solve complex tasks. Agent skills can be inherently divided into general skills for broad cognitive transfer and task-specific skills for dynamic execution. However, existing skill-based reinforcement learning (RL) methods typically force a rigid choice between full externalization, which incurs prohibitive context overhead, and full internalization, which risks overfitting and knowledge conflicts. To address this dilemma, we propose Skill0.5, a novel agentic RL framework that explicitly differentiates skill treatments by combining general skill internalization with task-specific skill utilization. Driven by a dynamic, difficulty-aware router, Skill0.5 streams tasks into distinct mastery tiers to apply tailored optimization strategies: it internalizes general skills via privileged distillation to build a cognitive foundation for hard tasks, while using diagnostic probing on easy tasks to penalize shortcuts and enforce specific skill utilization. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop demonstrate that Skill0.5 outperforms both memory-based and skill-based RL baselines, yielding performance improvements across both in-distribution and out-of-distribution scenarios.


### [79] [Roles with Rails: Contract-Preserving Role Evolution in Multi-Agent Structured Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28433)
*Ling-Yue Ge, Lan-Zhe Guo*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出SERO框架，通过合约保持的角色演化机制，在LLM多智能体系统中实现自适应角色池扩展，在保持能力覆盖、通信兼容性、验证、聚合和输出协议五类结构合约不变的前提下优化任务性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有基于角色的LLM多智能体系统在适应性上面临两难困境：固定角色库丧失灵活性，而无约束的角色生成则会导致角色漂移，移除必要的结构性角色并破坏答案合约。已有方法未能解决角色演化过程中必须保留的结构性义务问题。

**Method:** SERO框架通过三类核心机制实现合约保持的角色演化：信用引导检索机制从打字角色卡池中选取子集、信用排序的通信DAG配合受保护终端聚合器与条件验证器修复机制、以及上下文赌博控制器驱动LLM提出编辑提案，仅在提案保持五类结构合约（能力覆盖、通信兼容性、验证、聚合、输出协议）且提升任务分数时才予以采纳。

**Result:** 在多个真实世界推理基准上，使用三种不同LLM主干网络的实验验证了合约保持的角色演化方法的有效性，表明SERO相比固定角色库或无约束生成方法在任务性能上取得显著提升。

**Conclusion:** 本文揭示了角色演化不仅仅是提示工程问题，而需要严格保持结构性合约。SERO框架为自适应LLM多智能体系统提供了一种可行范式，未来可进一步探索合约自动发现与角色间高阶交互。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Role-based LLM multi-agent systems need adaptive role pools, yet adapting such systems is not merely a matter of prompt optimization: roles often carry structural obligations, including capability coverage, message compatibility, validation, final-answer aggregation, and parser-compatible output protocols. Existing systems either fix the role inventory and lose adaptivity, or allow unconstrained generation to induce role drift, removing structurally necessary roles and breaking answer contracts. We formulate this as contract-preserving role evolution, requiring every committed edit to preserve five structural contracts (capability, communication, validation, aggregation, output protocol). We instantiate this formulation in SERO, a Self-Evolving Role Orchestration framework that evolves a typed role-card pool through credit-guided retrieval, a credit-ranked communication DAG with a protected terminal aggregator and conditional validator repair, and a contextual-bandit controller whose LLM-proposed edits are committed only when they preserve the contracts and improve task score. Experiments on real-world reasoning benchmarks across three LLM backbones confirm the value of contract-preserving role evolution.


### [80] [AdaDPO: Self-Adaptive Direct Preference Optimization with Balanced Gradient Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28440)
*Shaolong Chen, Madalina Ciobanu, Qingqing Mao, Ritankar Das*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
AdaDPO 提出一种自适应性 DPO 变体，通过基于 policy 模型生成概率的 stop-gradient 系数来均衡偏好与非偏好样本的梯度幅值，消除 DPO 中梯度不对称问题，在 AlpacaEval 2 上以极简代码改动实现更优对齐效果，且可泛化至多种对比偏好损失函数。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有 DPO 算法存在梯度不对称问题：损失函数抑制非偏好回答的速度远快于促进偏好回答，导致模型偏向学习回避错误答案而非生成优质答案，限制了偏好对齐的优化效率与生成质量。

**Method:** AdaDPO 在每个偏好对上引入基于 policy 模型生成概率的 stop-gradient 系数，参考模型概率作为可选组件，以此强制偏好概率与不偏好概率的梯度幅值相等；实际实现通过平衡逐 token 梯度并施加数值裁剪界以保持训练稳定性，同时保留 DPO 原有超参数结构，仅需数行代码改动。

**Result:** 在 Llama-3-8B-Instruct 上使用 UltraFeedback 并采用 SimPO 类似设置训练，AdaDPO 在 AlpacaEval 2 上优于 DPO：81% 超参数组合下获得更高长度控制胜率（LC），全局最佳 LC 达 48.3%、raw 胜率 46.1%，并在 88% 组合中扩大 LC 与 raw WR 的差距，有效缓解长度偏差；KL 散度、奖励边际与奖励准确率分析进一步证实其纠正梯度不平衡并实现更高效优化。

**Conclusion:** AdaDPO 纯损失层面的自适应机制可直接嵌入现有偏好对齐流程，无需更改数据采集或模型架构，且其自适应性原则可泛化至 SimPO、R-DPO、IPO、CPO 和 ORPO 等成对对比偏好损失族，具有广泛适用性与极低部署成本。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
DPO has become a widely adopted alternative to RLHF for aligning LLMs with human preferences, eliminating the need for a separate reward model or RL loop. Recent theoretical analysis uncovers an asymmetric gradient behavior in DPO: the loss suppresses dispreferred responses substantially faster than it promotes preferred ones, causing the model to learn to avoid bad answers rather than to generate good ones. We propose AdaDPO, a Self-Adaptive variant of the DPO algorithm that introduces per-preference-pair, stop-gradient-based coefficients derived directly from the policy model's generation probabilities, with the reference model's probabilities as an optional component. AdaDPO is constructed to enforce equality of gradient magnitudes between preferred and dispreferred probabilities; the practical implementation balances per-token gradients and applies a numerical clipping bound for stability, while retaining DPO's original hyperparameter structure. On Llama-3-8B-Instruct trained on UltraFeedback under a SimPO similar setup, AdaDPO consistently outperforms DPO on AlpacaEval 2: it achieves higher length-controlled win rates (LC) in 81% of hyperparameter combinations, attains the global best LC (48.3%) and raw win rate (46.1%), and enlarges the LC-over-WR margin in 88% of combinations, indicating effective mitigation of length bias. Additional analyses on KL divergence, reward margin, and reward accuracy confirm that AdaDPO rectifies the gradient imbalance and yields more efficient optimization. Because it operates purely at the loss level, AdaDPO can be dropped into existing preference-based alignment pipelines without changing data collection or model architectures. The method requires only a few lines of code, and the same self-adaptive principle generalizes to a broad family of pairwise contrastive preference losses including SimPO, R-DPO, IPO, CPO, and ORPO.


### [81] [Beyond One Path: Evaluating and Enhancing Divergent Thinking in Interactive LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28465)
*Jihyeong Park, Ingeol Baek, Jeonghyun Park, Hwanhee Lee*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出MUTATE基准，用于评估大语言模型在交互式设定下的发散性思维，并揭示其在即时收敛压力下的动作固化缺陷；同时提出ReDNA方法，通过分离无约束发散生成与收敛约束选择，显著提升agent在路径级和动作级两个维度的发散推理能力。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有LLM创造力评估将模型视为单轮文本生成器，无法捕捉agent在交互式迭代推理过程中的发散性思维能力；此外，传统评价仅关注成功路径，忽略了偏离路径的发散推理尝试。

**Method:** 提出MUTATE交互式基准，从路径级（发现多条替代路径到达同一目标）和动作级（非典型对象使用与机制转换）两个维度评估agent发散思维；同时提出ReDNA方法，将无约束的发散候选生成与收敛约束选择过程相分离，以克服即时收敛压力下的动作固化问题。

**Result:** MUTATE评估显示，前沿LLM在面对即时收敛压力时会出现动作固化，无法改善动作级发散性；ReDNA在路径级和动作级两个发散维度上均显著优于先前方法，并能有效泛化到外部创造力环境中；其成功源于增强的韧性发散推理能力，而非简单的环境探索。

**Conclusion:** 实验揭示了现有LLM创造力评估框架的结构性盲点——即时收敛压力会导致动作固化，而ReDNA通过分离发散生成与收敛选择过程能有效缓解该问题，为提升agent化发散推理能力提供了新方向。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Divergent thinking is a core dimension of creativity, yet existing evaluations of Large Language Models (LLMs) treat them as single-turn text generations, failing to capture how an agent reasons through iterative interaction. To address this, we introduce MUTATE, an interactive benchmark designed to evaluate agentic divergent thinking at two levels: path-level, where an agent discovers multiple alternative paths to the same goal, and action-level, where individual actions require non-typical, mechanism-shifting object uses. Unlike success-only evaluations, MUTATE scores both completed paths and off-path attempts, capturing divergent reasoning that conventional success rates discard. Our experiments with frontier LLMs reveal a structural blind spot in existing frameworks: when exposed to immediate convergence pressure, they tend to fall into immediate action fixation, failing to improve action-level divergence. To overcome this, we propose ReDNA, which separates unconstrained divergent candidate generation from convergent constraint selection. ReDNA significantly outperforms prior methods across both divergence levels and generalizes effectively to an external creativity environment. We also confirm its success stems from a qualitative enhancement of resilient divergent reasoning rather than simple environmental exploration.


### [82] [ClinicalEncoder26AM: A Multlilingual Diagnosable ColBERT Model; Evidences from the MultiClinNER Shared Task](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28521)
*François Remy*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
ClinicalEncoder26AM 是一个多语言临床文本编码器，通过多层级语义对齐、多适配器蒸馏和 ColBERT 式检索目标进行后训练，在 MultiClinNER 共享任务中通过轻量级 CNN 分类头微调后，在多语言实体召回和字符加权 F1 上取得了领先性能，且数据效率显著优于基础模型。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有临床文本编码模型在多语言场景下语义对齐能力不足，且缺乏同时利用命名实体级别和句子级别表示进行高效蒸馏的方法，导致下游信息抽取任务（如命名实体识别）对大量标注数据依赖性强、跨语言泛化能力有限。

**Method:** 该模型基于 BGE-M3 进行后训练，提出多层级语义对齐策略：将 token 级语义与临床潜在空间 ClinicalMap25（受 BioLORD-2023 启发，经合成与标注监督增强）对齐；结合合成临床笔记、医患对话及 MedMentions 等标注资源，采用多适配器蒸馏同时处理命名实体级和句子级表示，并引入 ColBERT 风格检索目标；在 MultiClinNER 任务中微调为 BIO 标注器，使用轻量级两层 CNN 头增强局部边界检测，支持单次 8192 token 窗口处理。

**Result:** 该模型在 MultiClinNER 共享任务中实现了多语言实体召回的最优结果（state-of-the-art），在所有实体类型和语言上的字符加权 F1 分数中位列 Top 5；训练曲线显示 ClinicalEncoder26AM 在数据效率上显著优于基础 BGE-M3 模型，验证了临床后训练对下游信息抽取的有效性。

**Conclusion:** ClinicalEncoder26AM 证明了多层级语义对齐与多适配器蒸馏策略能够有效提升临床文本表示的数据效率和跨语言泛化能力，为多语言医学信息抽取提供了一种简单且高性能的基线方案，其公开模型资源有利于推动该领域进一步研究。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
ClinicalEncoder26AM is a multilingual Diagnosable ColBERT for clinical and biomedical texts, which aligns at multiple levels its token-level semantic with ClinicalMap25, a clinical latent space inspired by BioLORD-2023 and enriched with synthetic and annotated supervision. The post-training recipe builds upon BGE-M3, and combines synthetic clinical notes, patient--doctor conversations, and annotated resources such as MedMentions, while considering both named-entity-level and sentence-level representations in a multi-adapter distillation, along with a ColBERT-style retrieval objective. In this system demonstration paper, we evaluate the model in the MultiClinNER shared task by finetuning it as a BIO tagger for patient symptoms, disorders, and procedure spans, using a lightweight two-layer CNN head to improve local boundary detection. The resulting system remains simple, processes most documents in a single 8192-token window, and achieves state-of-the-art multilingual entity recall, while achieving Top 5 overall across all entity types and languages in Character-weighted F1 scores. Training curves further show that ClinicalEncoder26AM is markedly more data-efficient than the base M3 model, supporting the usefulness of its clinical post-training for downstream information extraction.
  The model can be downloaded on https://huggingface.co/Parallia/ClinicalEncoder26AM-Diagnosable-Colbert-L2-for-multilingual-medical-texts


### [83] [GUI-CIDER: Mid-training GUI Agents via Causal Internalization and Density-aware Exemplar Reselection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28534)
*Zheng Wu, Chengcheng Han, Zhengxi Lu, Tianjie Ju, Yanyu Chen, Qi Gu, Xunliang Cai, Zhuosheng Zhang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
GUI-CIDER提出了一种中期训练方法，通过因果内化与密度感知样本重选，使多模态大语言模型显式学习GUI操作的世界知识，在知识理解和任务完成基准上均取得一致提升。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有GUI智能体在真实任务中受限于缺乏GUI操作世界知识，现有解决方案要么依赖昂贵的多智能体框架，要么采用SFT或RL等后训练范式，但后训练仅能通过动作标注或奖励信号隐式吸收知识，导致低效的轨迹记忆而非真正理解，因此亟需一种显式学习GUI世界知识的方法。

**Method:** GUI-CIDER包含三个阶段：(1) 数据合成，从GUI轨迹中蒸馏出静态规划知识和动态因果知识并转化为文本；(2) 样本重选，通过奖励因果结构并惩罚语义冗余来过滤语料；(3) 中期训练，使用精炼数据将所学知识嵌入模型参数中。

**Result:** 在两个GUI知识基准和三个任务完成基准上的大量实验表明，GUI-CIDER一致性地提升了智能体对GUI操作的理解能力和任务成功率。

**Conclusion:** GUI-CIDER通过中期训练的方式让模型显式学习GUI世界知识，避免了后训练中隐式记忆轨迹的局限，为构建真正理解GUI操作的智能体提供了有效路径，代码已开源。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Despite the rapid progress of multimodal large language models in building Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents, their real-world task completion is fundamentally bottlenecked by a lack of world knowledge about GUI operations. Existing solutions typically rely on expensive multi-agent scaffolding or conventional post-training paradigms, such as Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL). However, post-training only allows agents to implicitly absorb world knowledge through action annotations or reward signals, leading to inefficient trajectory memorization rather than genuine comprehension. Therefore, an approach that enables explicit learning of this knowledge is imperative. To this end, we propose GUI-CIDER, a mid-training method that explicitly internalizes GUI world knowledge through Causal Internalization and Density-aware Exemplar Reselection. GUI-CIDER operates in three stages: (1) data synthesis, which distills static planning and dynamic causal knowledge from GUI trajectories into text; (2) exemplar reselection, which filters the corpus by rewarding causal structures and penalizing semantic redundancy; and (3) mid-training, where the refined data is used to embed the acquired knowledge. Extensive experiments on two GUI knowledge benchmarks and three task completion benchmarks demonstrate that GUI-CIDER consistently improves both the agent's understanding of GUI operations and its task success rates.The codes are available at https://github.com/Wuzheng02/GUI-CIDER.


### [84] [GraphLit: Learning Text-Enriched Dynamic Character Network Representations for Literary Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28643)
*Gaspard Michel, Elena V. Epure, Romain Hennequin, Christophe Cerisara, Mirella Lapata*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出动态异质角色网络（DHCNs）将长篇小说组织为时间局部化的异质图，对齐角色与其文本语境，并设计自监督框架GraphLit通过掩码图自编码器学习丰富的文学表示，在12个角色相关任务上超越纯文本和纯图基线。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有文学文本的图表示方法主要聚焦于角色交互网络，忽略了角色交互发生的文本语境这一关键维度，导致无法捕捉角色关系与叙事上下文的深层关联。

**Method:** 引入动态异质角色网络（DHCNs），将长篇小说按时间窗口分割为局部异质图，同时建模角色节点和文本语境节点；从Project Gutenberg提取约20,000个DHCNs，并提出自监督学习框架GraphLit，采用掩码图自编码器目标进行表示学习。

**Result:** 在12个角色相关任务上，GraphLit相较纯文本和纯图基线均有提升，尤其在需要上下文理解的任务上优势显著；进一步通过分析叙事非线性和动态社交特征的关联，验证了DHCNs和GraphLit在文学分析中的实用性。

**Conclusion:** 融合文本语境的异质图表示与自监督图学习能够更有效地建模文学叙事中的角色关系，为计算文学分析提供了新的框架和工具。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Methods to represent literary texts as graphs or sequences of graphs mainly focus on representing character interactions, and often overlook another crucial aspect: the textual context in which characters interact. We introduce Dynamic Heterogeneous Character Networks (DHCNs), which organize long novels into temporally localized heterogeneous graphs that align characters with their textual contexts. We extract around 20,000 DHCNs from Project Gutenberg, and propose GraphLit, a self-supervised learning framework that learns rich literary representations through a masked graph autoencoder objective. Across a wide-range of 12 character-related tasks, GraphLit improves over text-only and graph-only baselines, particularly on tasks requiring contextual understanding. Finally, we demonstrate the applicability of DHCNs and GraphLit for literary analysis by studying the link between narrative non-linearity and dynamic social features.


### [85] [Rethinking Memory as Continuously Evolving Connectivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28773)
*Jizhan Fang, Buqiang Xu, Zhixian Wang, Haoliang Cao, Xinle Deng, Baohua Dong, Hangcheng Zhu, Ruohui Huang, Gang Yu, Ying Wei, Guozhou Zheng, Feiyu Xiong, Haofen Wang, Huajun Chen, Ningyu Zhang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
FluxMem 提出一种连通性演化的记忆框架，将记忆建模为异构图并通过初始连接、反馈驱动精炼和长期巩固三个阶段逐步优化拓扑结构，在多个基准上取得SOTA性能，解决了动态智能体环境中静态记忆系统鲁棒性不足的问题。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有记忆增强型LLM智能体通常将记忆视为静态仓库，使用预定义表示和固定检索管道，无法在动态智能体环境中适应反馈、任务变化和异质信号对记忆内容和连接方式的持续重塑需求，缺乏灵活演化的能力。

**Method:** FluxMem 将记忆建模为异构图，通过三个阶段逐步优化图拓扑：初始连接形成、反馈驱动的精炼以及长期巩固。执行过程中，框架修复缺失链接、剪枝干扰、对齐抽象粒度，并将反复成功的轨迹蒸馏为可复用的过程化通路，由记忆通用性和演化成熟度两个指标进行引导。

**Result:** 在LoCoMo、Mind2Web和GAIA三个不同类型的基准上，FluxMem 均取得了一致的SOTA性能，在复杂智能体环境中展现出强大的自适应能力和泛化性能。

**Conclusion:** 该研究证实了记忆拓扑动态演化对于提升LLM智能体在复杂动态环境中适应性和通用性的关键作用，并为未来智能体记忆系统的设计提供了可借鉴的图演化框架和评估指标。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Existing memory-augmented LLM agents often treat memory as a static repository with pre-defined representations and fixed retrieval pipelines, which is brittle in dynamic agentic environments where feedback, task variation, and heterogeneous signals continuously reshape what should be remembered and how it should be connected. To address this, we propose FluxMem, a connectivity-evolving memory framework that models memory as a heterogeneous graph and progressively refines its topology through three stages: initial connection formation, feedback-driven refinement, and long-term consolidation. During execution, FluxMem repairs missing links, prunes interference, aligns abstraction granularity, and distills recurrent successful trajectories into reusable procedural circuits, guided by one metric for memory generalizability and evolutionary maturity. Across three fundamentally distinct benchmarks including LoCoMo, Mind2Web, and GAIA, FluxMem achieves consistent state-of-the-art performance, demonstrating strong adaptation and generalization in complex agentic environments. The code will be open-sourced in https://github.com/zjunlp/LightMem.


### [86] [Agent Explorative Policy Optimization for Multimodal Agentic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28774)
*Minki Kang, Shizhe Diao, Ryo Hachiuma, Sung Ju Hwang, Pavlo Molchanov, Yu-Chiang Frank Wang, Byung-Kwan Lee*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出AXPO算法，通过在工具使用失败时保留思考前缀并重采样工具调用及后续生成，配合不确定性驱动的前缀选择，有效弥补了智能体推理中思考与行动之间的不对称性，在九个多模态基准上超越SFT+GRPO，且8B模型在Pass@4上超过32B基座模型。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 视觉语言模型在复杂推理任务上表现出色，但许多实际问题需要借助外部工具，而内部推理本身无法解决。现有方法如GRPO无法有效处理智能体推理中思考（thinking）与工具使用（tool use）之间的结构性不对称——工具使用仅出现在约30%的rollout中，且当所有使用工具的rollout均错误时（约占40%的问题），学习信号被抑制。

**Method:** 提出AXPO（Agent eXplorative Policy Optimization）算法，针对每个全错的工具使用子组，固定思考前缀（thinking prefix），重新采样工具调用及其后续生成，并采用基于不确定性的前缀选择策略，从而增强工具调用位置的学习信号。

**Result:** 在九个多模态基准和三种规模的Qwen3-VL-Thinking上，SFT+AXPO在平均性能上优于SFT+GRPO（8B模型Pass@1平均提升1.8个百分点，Pass@4提升1.8个百分点）；8B模型的SFT+AXPO在Pass@4上以仅四分之一的参数量超越了32B基座模型。

**Conclusion:** AXPO通过针对性地重采样工具使用失败案例并固定思考前缀，有效缓解了思考与行动之间的不对称性带来的训练信号抑制问题，为智能体推理中工具使用的强化学习训练提供了更高效的优化方案，且在小模型上展现出显著的计算效率优势。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision-language models with extended reasoning succeed on complex problems, but many real-world problems require external tools that internal reasoning alone often cannot resolve. Agentic reasoning therefore interleaves two behaviors with a structural asymmetry: thinking (the self-contained default) and tool use (a high-variance auxiliary acting). We refer to this asymmetry as the Thinking-Acting Gap. Under standard RL recipes like GRPO, the gap manifests as two diagnostic symptoms during training: tool use is attempted on only ~30% of rollouts, and when attempted, the tool-using rollouts within a group are all-wrong on ~40% of questions, suppressing the learning signal at the tool calls that needed it. We propose AXPO (Agent eXplorative Policy Optimization): for each all-wrong tool-using subgroup, AXPO fixes the thinking prefix and resamples the tool call and its continuation, paired with uncertainty-based prefix selection. Across nine multimodal benchmarks and three scales of Qwen3-VL-Thinking, SFT+AXPO outperforms SFT+GRPO at average (+1.8pp Pass@1 and +1.8pp Pass@4 at 8B on average) and 8B with SFT+AXPO surpasses the 32B Base on Pass@4 with 4 times fewer parameters.


### [87] [The Abstraction Gap in Vision-Language Causal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28779)
*Chinh Hoang, Mohammad Rashedul Hasan*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出双探针方法（文本探针和链式文本探针）及抽象差距（AG）指标，构建CAGE基准（49500个问题，涵盖Pearl因果层次），系统评估八种视觉语言模型（VLM）的因果推理忠实性，发现大多数模型存在显著AG（>0.50），但特定模型可实现近零AG，表明该能力取决于预训练和架构选择。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有对视觉语言模型（VLM）的评估无法区分其生成流畅语言的能力与进行真正因果推理的能力，缺乏将语言合理性从忠实因果推理中分离出来的诊断工具。

**Method:** 提出双探针方法学：文本探针（Text-Only Probe）测量语言质量，链式文本探针（Chain-Text Probe）要求模型先生成显式因果链再作答；基于两者分数计算抽象差距（AG）指标以量化归一化性能差异；构建CAGE基准，包含5500张图像上的49500个问题，覆盖Pearl因果层次。

**Result:** 在八种VLM上的评估显示，七种模型的AG超过0.50，文本分数达6–8分而链式分数低于2.5分；使用45000个链注释样本进行微调未能缩小该差距；但有一个模型实现了近零AG，表明因果推理能力存在于当前VLM架构中。

**Conclusion:** VLM的忠实因果推理能力并非不可实现，而是取决于预训练和架构选择；CAGE可作为诊断VLM因果推理忠实性的有效工具；仅靠大规模链注释微调不足以弥合抽象差距。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision-language models (VLMs) generate fluent causal explanations, but current evaluations cannot distinguish linguistic plausibility from faithful causal reasoning. We introduce a dual-probe methodology that isolates these properties. The Text-Only Probe measures linguistic quality. The Chain-Text Probe requires models to first generate explicit causal chains. The Abstraction Gap (AG) metric quantifies the normalized performance difference. Evaluating eight VLMs on CAGE (Causal Abstraction Gap Evaluation), a benchmark of 49,500 questions across 5,500 images spanning Pearl's causal hierarchy, we find seven models exhibit AG exceeding 0.50 with text scores of 6--8 but chain scores below 2.5. Fine-tuning on 45,000 chain-annotated examples fails to close the gap. However, one model achieves near-zero AG. The capability exists within current VLM architectures and depends on pretraining and architectural choices. CAGE provides a diagnostic tool for assessing faithful causal reasoning in VLMs.


### [88] [VLMs May Not Globally Enhance Human Alignment over LLMs During Natural Reading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28818)
*Jinzhou Wu, Zhengwu Ma, Jixing Li, Baoping Tang, Zitong Lu*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文通过严格控制文本输入条件，对比匹配的LLM和VLM对自然阅读中全脑fMRI和眼动数据的对齐程度，发现多模态预训练并未带来全局性的人类对齐优势，但在视觉语义丰富的句子中显示出选择性优势。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 视觉-语言学习是否能使文本表示在自然阅读过程中更接近人类大脑处理模式尚不明确，以往研究常将多模态训练、在线视觉输入与跨模态融合等因素混在一起，难以隔离多模态预训练历史本身的独立影响。

**Method:** 研究对比了严格匹配的LLM与VLM对，在纯文本输入条件下评估其与人类自然阅读数据集的对齐程度，该数据集包含全脑fMRI响应和同步眼动追踪扫视数据，从而隔离多模态训练历史的影响，避免在线视觉输入或跨模态融合的干扰。

**Result:** 多模态预训练在自然阅读中并不赋予模型全局性的人类对齐优势，语言内部表征仍是建模人类文本处理的关键因素；但在包含较强视觉语义内容的句子中，VLM在fMRI和眼动对齐上均表现出选择性优势。

**Conclusion:** 多模态预训练对人类语言表征的贡献是选择性的而非全局性的，研究提供了一个受控的计算框架用于测试视觉学习历史如何塑造模型与人类在语言处理中的对齐。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have become increasingly useful computational models of human language processing, but it remains unclear whether vision-language learning makes text representations more human-like during natural reading. Here, we address this question by comparing tightly matched LLM and vision-language model (VLM) pairs under a strictly text-only setting, allowing us to isolate the effect of multimodal training history from online visual input or cross-modal fusion. We evaluate model alignment with a human natural-reading dataset that includes whole-cortex fMRI responses and synchronized eye-tracking saccades. Our findings demonstrate that multimodal pretraining may not confer a uniform, global advantage in human alignment during natural reading, indicating that language-internal representations remain the key factor for modeling human text processing. However, the VLM advantage could emerge more selectively when sentences contain stronger visual semantic content, with converging evidence from both fMRI and eye-movement alignments. Together, our findings provide a controlled in silico framework for testing how visual learning history shapes model-human alignment of language processing, suggesting that multimodal pretraining contributes selectively rather than globally to human-like language representations during natural reading.
